聯發科等6檔掰了</h1></section><p class="alr4vq1"><span class="signature">鉅亨網記者陳于晴 台北</span><span class="separator"></span><time dateTime="2025-06-03T11:21:38.000Z">2025-06-03 19:21</time></p><main id="article-container" class="c1tt5pk2" style="--c1tt5pk2-0:20px"><section style="margin-top:30px"><p>擁有 122 萬受益人、資產規模 3651 億元的群益台灣精選高息 ETF(<a href="https://www.cnyes.com/twstock/00919" target="_self" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-ga-target="news" data-ga-event-name="Click_Quote" data-ga-section="News_Article_文中行情" data-ga-click-item="TWS:00919:STOCK:ETF">00919-TW</a>) 換股秀登場，根據臺灣指數公司公布成分股調整資料顯示，本次新增 16 檔，其中，金控雙雄富邦及國泰皆入列，台灣市值前 50 大公司成分股增至 8 檔，而聯發科、京城銀等 6 檔則被刪除。最新調整自明 (4) 日起生效，定審異動的權重分配須在 8 個交易日內調整完畢。</p></section><p><div class="c1hvmcli"><figure><div class="iirgi4a"><img alt="cover image of news article" fetchPriority="high" decoding="async" data-nimg="fill" class="cr8g41v" 聯發科等6檔掰了。(圖:shutterstock)</figcaption></figure></div></p><section style="margin-top:30px">

</section><section style="margin-top:30px"><p>00919 追蹤指數每年調整 2 次成分股，此次新增 16 檔，分別為富邦金 (<a href="https://www.cnyes.com/twstock/2881" target="_self" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-ga-target="news" data-ga-event-name="Click_Quote" data-ga-section="News_Article_文中行情" data-ga-click-item="TWS:2881:STOCK:COMMON">2881-TW</a>)、國泰金 (<a href="https://www.cnyes.com/twstock/2882" target="_self" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-ga-target="news" data-ga-event-name="Click_Quote" data-ga-section="News_Article_文中行情" data-ga-click-item="TWS:2882:STOCK:COMMON">2882-TW</a>)、陽明 (<a href="https://www.cnyes.com/twstock/2609" target="_self" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-ga-target="news" data-ga-event-name="Click_Quote" data-ga-section="News_Article_文中行情" data-ga-click-item="TWS:2609:STOCK:COMMON">2609-TW</a>)、群光 (<a href="https://www.cnyes.com/twstock/2385" target="_self" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-ga-target="news" data-ga-event-name="Click_Quote" data-ga-section="News_Article_文中行情" data-ga-click-item="TWS:2385:STOCK:COMMON">2385-TW</a>)、可成 (<a href="https://www.cnyes.com/twstock/2474" target="_self" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-ga-target="news" data-ga-event-name="Click_Quote" data-ga-section="News_Article_文中行情" data-ga-click-item="TWS:2474:STOCK:COMMON">2474-TW</a>)、聚陽 (<a href="https://www.cnyes.com/twstock/1477" target="_self" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-ga-target="news" data-ga-event-name="Click_Quote" data-ga-section="News_Article_文中行情" data-ga-click-item="TWS:1477:STOCK:COMMON">1477-TW</a>)、大同 (<a href="https://www.cnyes.com/twstock/2371" target="_self" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-ga-target="news" data-ga-event-name="Click_Quote" data-ga-section="News_Article_文中行情" data-ga-click-item="TWS:2371:STOCK:COMMON">2371-TW</a>)、材料&nbsp; -KY(<a href="https://www.cnyes.com/twstock/4763" target="_self" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-ga-target="news" data-ga-event-name="Click_Quote" data-ga-section="News_Article_文中行情" data-ga-click-item="TWS:4763:STOCK:COMMON">4763-TW</a>)、美律 (2439)、義隆 (<a href="https://www.cnyes.com/twstock/2458" target="_self" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-ga-target="news" data-ga-event-name="Click_Quote" data-ga-section="News_Article_文中行情" data-ga-click-item="TWS:2458:STOCK:COMMON">2458-TW</a>)、順達 (<a href="https://www.cnyes.com/twstock/3211" target="_self" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-ga-target="news" data-ga-event-name="Click_Quote" data-ga-section="News_Article_文中行情" data-ga-click-item="TWS:3211:STOCK:COMMON">3211-TW</a>)、群電 (<a href="https://www.cnyes.com/twstock/6412" target="_self" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-ga-target="news" data-ga-event-name="Click_Quote" data-ga-section="News_Article_文中行情" data-ga-click-item="TWS:6412:STOCK:COMMON">6412-TW</a>)、長華 (<a href="https://www.cnyes.com/twstock/8070" target="_self" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-ga-target="news" data-ga-event-name="Click_Quote" data-ga-section="News_Article_文中行情" data-ga-click-item="TWS:8070:STOCK:COMMON">8070-TW</a>)、冠德 (<a href="https://www.cnyes.com/twstock/2520" target="_self" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-ga-target="news" data-ga-event-name="Click_Quote" data-ga-section="News_Article_文中行情" data-ga-click-item="TWS:2520:STOCK:COMMON">2520-TW</a>)、復盛應用 (<a href="https://www.cnyes.com/twstock/6670" target="_self" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-ga-target="news" data-ga-event-name="Click_Quote" data-ga-section="News_Article_文中行情" data-ga-click-item="TWS:6670:STOCK:COMMON">6670-TW</a>)、台灣虎航 (<a href="https://www.cnyes.com/twstock/6757" target="_self" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-ga-target="news" data-ga-event-name="Click_Quote" data-ga-section="News_Article_文中行情" data-ga-click-item="TWG:6757:STOCK:COMMON">6757-TW</a>)。</p></section><section>

</section><div id="div-gpt-ad-cnyes_news_article_middle_1" class="a1mzdm1v" style="--a1mzdm1v-0:728px;--a1mzdm1v-1:90px;--a1mzdm1v-2:728px;--a1mzdm1v-3:90px;--a1mzdm1v-4:32px;--a1mzdm1v-5:32px;--a1mzdm1v-6:auto;--a1mzdm1v-7:auto"><span aria-live="polite" aria-busy="true"><span class="react-loading-skeleton" style="border-radius:6px;width:100%;height:100%">‌</span><br/></span></div><section style="margin-top:30px"><p>同時刪除 6 檔成分股，分別為聯發科 (<a href="https://www.cnyes.com/twstock/2454" target="_self" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-ga-target="news" data-ga-event-name="Click_Quote" data-ga-section="News_Article_文中行情" data-ga-click-item="TWS:2454:STOCK:COMMON">2454-TW</a>)、京城銀 (<a href="https://www.cnyes.com/twstock/2809" target="_self" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-ga-target="news" data-ga-event-name="Click_Quote" data-ga-section="News_Article_文中行情" data-ga-click-item="TWS:2809:STOCK:COMMON">2809-TW</a>)、洋基工程 (<a href="https://www.cnyes.com/twstock/6691" target="_self" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-ga-target="news" data-ga-event-name="Click_Quote" data-ga-section="News_Article_文中行情" data-ga-click-item="TWG:6691:STOCK:COMMON">6691-TW</a>)、國票金 (<a href="https://www.cnyes.com/twstock/2889" target="_self" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-ga-target="news" data-ga-event-name="Click_Quote" data-ga-section="News_Article_文中行情" data-ga-click-item="TWS:2889:STOCK:COMMON">2889-TW</a>)、海悅 (<a href="https://www.cnyes.com/twstock/2348" target="_self" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-ga-target="news" data-ga-event-name="Click_Quote" data-ga-section="News_Article_文中行情" data-ga-click-item="TWS:2348:STOCK:COMMON">2348-TW</a>)、寶雅 (<a href="https://www.cnyes.com/twstock/5904" target="_self" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-ga-target="news" data-ga-event-name="Click_Quote" data-ga-section="News_Article_文中行情" data-ga-click-item="TWS:5904:STOCK:COMMON">5904-TW</a>)。</p></section><section style="margin-top:30px">

</section><section style="margin-top:30px"><p>ETF 理財達人表示，觀察 00919 的最新持股，在電子、傳產、航運、金融都配置一定的比例，具有分散風險的樣態，整體而言，提高投資人對持股的安心感，本次新增富邦金、國泰金與陽明，加計既有的中信金、長榮、長榮航、聯電、聯詠，市值前 50 大的成分股達 8 檔。</p></section><section style="margin-top:30px">

</section><section style="margin-top:30px"><p>而在產業配置上也趨於多元分散，最新產業分布以金融、半導體、航運類的高息成分股為主。</p></section><section style="margin-top:30px">

</section><section style="margin-top:30px"><p>市場法人表示，00919 成分股配置不僅看重現金股利率也看重成分股的市值規模以及長期成交量，必須要同時兼顧，新投組更符合投資人期待，也期待替 00919 再添股價上漲的動能與豐厚股利進帳。</p></section><section style="margin-top:30px">

</section><section style="margin-top:30px"><p>00919 第 9 次預估配息 0.72 元維持新高，預估 12.98% 年化配息率最高，也是唯一一檔配息維持新高的台股高息 ETF，連續 9 季年化配息率都逾 10% 優於投資人期待，配息表現在高息 ETF 中鶴立雞群。00919 除息日為 6 月 17 日，參與除息最後買進日為 6 月 16 日，配息發放日為 7 月 11 日，有興趣的投資人可多留意。</p></section><section style="margin-top:30px">

日，參與除息最後買進日為 6 月 16 日，配息發放日為 7 月 11
